GT Equivalence Verification (CRK16)

GT: -c0*A + c1*_f*A**c2
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed function (independent of \(t\)):
\[
f(A,t)=0.9709294495916855\,A^{1/3}-0.24581249010242617\,A.
\]
So any matching candidate must be reducible (by choosing its free constants) to exactly “(constant)\(\cdot A^{1/3}\) + (constant)\(\cdot A\)” with **no remaining \(t\)-dependence**, no extra powers of \(A\), no logs/exp/Abs artifacts, and no additive constant term.

### 1. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2\)
Combine linear terms: \(A(c1+c2)\). Choose \(c0=0.9709294495916855\), \(c1+c2=-0.24581249010242617\). Match.

### 2. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1\)
Directly match with \(c0=0.9709294495916855\), \(c1=-0.24581249010242617\). Match.

### 3. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^{1/3}c1 + Ac2\)
Combine \(A^{1/3}(c0+c1)\). Choose \(c0+c1=0.9709294495916855\), \(c2=-0.24581249010242617\). Match.

### 4. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^{1/3}c1 + A^{1/3}c2 + Ac3 + c4\)
Need no constant term: set \(c4=0\). Combine \(A^{1/3}(c0+c1+c2)\). Choose \(c0+c1+c2=0.9709294495916855\), \(c3=-0.24581249010242617\). Match.

### 5. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 + Ac3 + c4\)
Set \(c4=0\). Combine \(A(c1+c2+c3)\). Choose \(c0=0.9709294495916855\), \(c1+c2+c3=-0.24581249010242617\). Match.

### 6. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 + c3\)
Set \(c3=0\). Combine \(A(c1+c2)\). Choose \(c0=0.9709294495916855\), \(c1+c2=-0.24581249010242617\). Match.

### 7. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + Ac2 + Ac3 + Ac4 + c5\)
Set \(c5=0\). Combine \(A(c1+c2+c3+c4)\). Choose \(c0=0.9709294495916855\), sum \(=-0.24581249010242617\). Match.

### 8. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^{1/3}c1 + Ac2 + Ac3 + c4\)
Set \(c4=0\). Combine \(A^{1/3}(c0+c1)\) and \(A(c2+c3)\). Choose sums to match coefficients. Match.

### 9. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^{1/3}c1 + Ac2 + c3 + c4 e^{c5|Ac6+c7 t|}\)
To remove non-GT parts for all \(A,t\): set \(c4=0\) and \(c3=0\). Then reduce to case like (8) without \(Ac3\): choose \(c0+c1=0.9709...\), \(c2=-0.2458...\). Match.

### 10. \(A^{1/3}c0 + \dfrac{A c1}{(c2+t)^5} + Ac3 + c4\)
Must eliminate \(t\)-dependence: set \(c1=0\). Also set \(c4=0\). Then \(A^{1/3}c0+Ac3\) matches with \(c0=0.9709...\), \(c3=-0.2458...\). Match.

### 11. \(\frac{A^{1/3}c0}{c1+t^2}+\frac{A^{1/3}c2 t^2}{c1+t^2}+\frac{A c3 t^2}{c1+t^2}+\frac{A c4}{c1+t^2}\)
This is \(\frac{A^{1/3}(c0+c2 t^2)+A(c4+c3 t^2)}{c1+t^2}\), inherently \(t\)-dependent unless it collapses to a constant in \(t\). But numerator is at most linear in \(t^2\) while denominator is \(c1+t^2\); to make the ratio \(t\)-independent for all \(t\), you’d need numerator \(=(c1+t^2)\times(\alpha A^{1/3}+\beta A)\). That would require \(A^{1/3}\) coefficient to have a constant term \(\alpha c1\) and a \(t^2\) term \(\alpha\), similarly for \(A\). However numerator’s \(A^{1/3}\) part is \(c0+c2 t^2\) (no \(c1\) factor available unless you tie constants, but constants are free scalars not functions of \(c1\) in that way). You could set \(c0=\alpha c1\), \(c2=\alpha\), \(c4=\beta c1\), \(c3=\beta\). Then expression becomes exactly \(\alpha A^{1/3}+\beta A\) for all \(t\) (provided \(c1+t^2\neq 0\) but as functions they coincide where defined). So it *can* match. Choose \(\alpha=0.9709...\), \(\beta=-0.2458...\). Match.

### 12. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + A^{c2}c3 + c4 e^{A c5}\log(c6 t+1)\)
Eliminate extra terms: set \(c3=0\) and \(c4=0\). Then match with \(c0=0.9709...\), \(c1=-0.2458...\). Match.

### 13. \(A^{1/3}c0 + A^{1/3}c1 + Ac2 + c3\)

### 14. \(A^{1/3}c0 + Ac1 + c2\)
